# <a name="responsecode"></a><span data-ttu-id="d1576-103">ResponseCode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d1576-103">ResponseCode</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d1576-104">O elemento **ResponseCode** fornece informações de status sobre a solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d1576-104">The **ResponseCode** element provides status information about the request.</span></span> 
  
- [<span data-ttu-id="d1576-105">ResponseMessage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d1576-105">ResponseMessage</span></span>](responsemessage.md) 
- [<span data-ttu-id="d1576-106">ResponseCode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d1576-106">ResponseCode</span></span>](responsecode.md)
  
```XML
<ResponseCode/>
```

<span data-ttu-id="d1576-107">**ResponseCodeType**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d1576-107">**ResponseCodeType**</span></span>

## <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="d1576-1480">Comentários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d1576-1480">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d1576-1481">Este elemento não é necessário e não está incluído em todas as respostas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d1576-1481">This element is not required and is not included in all responses.</span></span> 
  
<span data-ttu-id="d1576-1482">O esquema que descreve este elemento está localizado no diretório virtual do IIS que hospeda os Serviços Web do Exchange.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d1576-1482">The schema that describes this element is located in the IIS virtual directory that hosts Exchange Web Services.</span></span>
